SRC2290112198
On November 17, 2022, we denied your Form I-485, Application to Register Permanent Residence or Adjust Status, Receipt Number SRC2290112198. We sent you a denial notice that explains why we denied your case and your options. Please follow the instructions in the notice. If you do not receive your denial notice by December 2, 2022, please go to www.uscis.gov/e-request to request a copy of the notice. If you move, go to www.uscis.gov/addresschange to give us your new mailing address.
